Verify That Error Is Encountered When Invalid Token Is Used
    [Tags]    functional
    Create Test Variables For Exchange Order India
    Send Exchange Order Post Request For India    token=12345.12345.12345    status_code=401
    Verify Exchange Order Is Not Saved
    Create Test Variables For Exchange Order India
    Send Exchange Order Post Request For India    token=abcde.abcde.abcde    status_code=401
    Verify Exchange Order Is Not Saved
    Create Test Variables For Exchange Order India
    Send Exchange Order Post Request For India    token=!@#$%^&*().!@#$%^&*().!@#$%^&*()    status_code=401
    Verify Exchange Order Is Not Saved
